  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_21a5d63d-c04d-4c6e-948a-f74cea34d8f1'

  <span id="freeText13847511725086592406" style="display:none">What happens when destiny wants to bring two people together? And what happens when one of them accepts this as a gift of God, while the other refuses to bow down to destiny? <br /> <br />Ved, a young man who climbed the success ladder with sheer hard work and determination, is as attached to his roots as ever. A humble, helpful and gentle soul who is loved by all…except by the one woman he loves with all his heart. <br /> <br />Maya, a young and vivacious girl, who has been challenged by fate time and again. From being left motherless at the tender age of three, to being shunned by her family at 22, Maya didn’t have it easy. <br /> <br />While Ved opens his heart for Maya, she makes it clear to him that the only feeling she will ever have for him is hatred. <br /> <br />Come and embark on this journey of emotions, misunderstandings, love...and be a part of their emotional rollercoaster ride. <br /> <br /> <br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3328739897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3130305347073491938">There are some stories which you want to end reading and then there are some which crave for more. Well, this book falls in the latter category.<br/> <br/>Well, if there is a thing called, don't judge a book by its cover, then it completely goes with this book. The book cover isn't that eye-catching but trusts me once you start reading it, you will get into Ved-Maya's world.<br/><br/>The book has a story of love, an eternal love which started from a small misunderstanding. Coming to the story, Ved's family is seeki</span>
  <span id="freeText3130305347073491938" style="display:none">There are some stories which you want to end reading and then there are some which crave for more. Well, this book falls in the latter category.<br /> <br />Well, if there is a thing called, don't judge a book by its cover, then it completely goes with this book. The book cover isn't that eye-catching but trusts me once you start reading it, you will get into Ved-Maya's world.<br /><br />The book has a story of love, an eternal love which started from a small misunderstanding. Coming to the story, Ved's family is seeking a beautiful bride for Ved. Then they get informed about Radhika but while going to meet with Radhika, Ved meets Maya. Well, how and when you can read that in the book.<br />Let me tell you what I really felt about the book. Have you ever waited for someone for years? If yes, then you know how it feels. This book has love, love and some more love. <br /><br />The author has beautifully described not just only romance between two couples, but also how a simple misunderstanding can create havoc in someone's life. Not just that, even after getting committed, there are a lot of things which can lead to a breakup. <br /><br />VedMaya is a saga of love. The review is getting longer and I need to stop. Well even if you are not a fan of romance genre book, this book will change your conception of love. <br /><br />Witnessing the journey of Ved-Maya, I cried, smiled and felt being loved. <br /><br />Go get it guys. Highly recommended.</span>

  <span id="freeText986609755095822533" style="display:none"><strong>Loved it..</strong><br /><br />I have read Vineeta's Nameless Encounter and loved every bit of it. It still remains on top among my favorite books. This one has been pending since a very long time. Finally got a chance to read it yesterday. Yes.. I started n couldn't keep it down. Had to just finish it. I am not a writer n don't have different ways of writing- I loved this. Yes I truly loved this. Ved n Maya- Ved's persistent love, Maya's persistent hatred; Ved's patience, Maya's temper,, to Maya's love .. loved going through their journey .. Thank you Vineeta for this. Now that I think of it, I would love to read more about Vikram and Naina as well as Priyanka and Raghu .. I am sure they have wonderful stories to tell. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FthrYE2zitzeaRsyR1xmEh5jvLsseGx5+6/jd1GPwlclfP7y9XjXatiOHxTDFsLk++S1zj84P0W/jV5m2XmUxQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5YvWLhUTLeBHFPeRxeo0DfAfWk3tZf0/PkWlnRTP4WnWL0O8rdhwVkHz87dBoJD7FZhTOP4lrgN6ZxiMnDm3+w==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
